href='/Writing/183434?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送李主簿夷行之官河阴四首<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span id='poem_sentence_0_183571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183571'>戍期良敦迫，王畿方滞淫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183571'>疲筋苦跧卧，行药<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>长川阴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183571'>云物接平陆，不见西飞禽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183571'>风从城阙来，如闻钟漏音。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183571'>昕霁更东迈，区区子牟心。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183537_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183537'>舟人惊<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>朝鼓，敛繂逗长林。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183537_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183537'>林端落滞雪，沙际起鸣禽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183537_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183537'>病客坐长叹，摄衣涕流襟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183537_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183537'>亲朋自兹远，可是慕山阴。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183537_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183537'>兴尽莫回楫，何人知此心。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183537_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_183538_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183538'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183538'>沄沄清川流，冉冉浮云阴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183538_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183538'>天寒日云莫，鱼鸟方潜沈。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183538_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183538'>吾岂厌安隐，东浮违宿心。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183538_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183538'>一官未足养，老境行侵寻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183538_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183538'>牛歌感白石，马骨要黄金。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183538_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183538'>惭无子虚作，万里悬知音。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183538_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183538'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_183538_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年11月</a>　是年十一月,赴和州任管界巡检,舟次陈留有诗。作品：《留侯庙下作》<div id='poem_183689' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183689' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183689?labeling=true' target='_blank'>留侯庙下作<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183689")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183689_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183689_0'>① 按留侯本封沛国之留城，今古祠存焉。晋义熙中，宋公镇徐，尝下教修缮，今祠中石刻虽破裂，犹可识。余官彭城日，欲赋一诗，匆匆（原作忽忽，据清抄本改）不暇及。丁卯冬，沿洛东下，阻冰于陈留，舟次有神祠，特严邃，榜曰汉留侯庙，盖邑人误谓侯封为陈留也。余时抱病（清抄本、四库本作疾）殊困，因默有祷焉。岁暮疾平，赋此诗，具冠笏拜谒，高吟神坐前，偿宿志也。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183689'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183689'>文成念韩痛，破产伺强秦。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183689'>千金募健士，椎断属车尘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183689'>东去变名姓，浮游淮泗滨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183689'>忍耻奉遗履，得书何老人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183689'>十年风云会，赤帝资经纶。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183689'>鸿门祸端结，一言即解纷。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183689'>英彭既合纵，楚项提孤军。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183689'>伟哉借箸谈，竖儒无复陈。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183689'>分疆饵两将，来若从龙云。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183689'>释怨俾侯印，谋销蛇豕群。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_183689'>定都天府国，推功归奉春。<div id='poem_sentence_10_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_183689'>四老落吾术，拂巾辞隐沦。<div id='poem_sentence_11_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_183689'>东朝羽翼就，楚调徒悲辛。<div id='poem_sentence_12_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_183689'>出处能事毕，致君终乞身。<div id='poem_sentence_13_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_183689'>岂眷万户封，仅与萧酂均。<div id='poem_sentence_14_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_183689'>淮阴败晚节，顾亦非吾伦。<div id='poem_sentence_15_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_183689'>愿访赤松子，逍遥云汉津。<div id='poem_sentence_16_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_183689'>强饭示终殁，爽灵方上宾。<div id='poem_sentence_17_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_183689'>严祠镇川湄，馀泽及斯民。<div id='poem_sentence_18_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_183689'>客子老将至，低回冗从臣。<div id='poem_sentence_19_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_183689'>惭无应时策，肝膈空轮囷。<div id='poem_sentence_20_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_183689'>可教固无类，慨然辄求伸。<div id='poem_sentence_21_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_183689'>未<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集作祇）</span>应终万古，黄石独能<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集作共威）</span>神。<div id='poem_sentence_22_183689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_183689'></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_183689_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年2月</a>　去年冬,阻雪陈留,是年二月方行,有诗。作品：《陈留南城马上简李公年》<div id='poem_183389' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183389' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183389?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈留南城马上简李公年<span class='inlineComment2'>（李字之茂。戊辰二月赋）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183389")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_183389_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183389'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183389'>南郭何人卜筑幽，平田高树带清沟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183389_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183389'>隔墙野鸟啼晴昼，驻马行人照白头。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183389_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》（124册）卷二六七三载此文,上海辞书出版社 安徽教育出版社2006年版第51页。）</span><div id='poem_1206402' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1206402' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1206402?labeling=true' target='_blank'>校吕氏春秋记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1092年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_1206402")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1206402_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1206402'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1206402'>右《吕氏春秋》，总二十六卷，凡百六十篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1206402_comment'></div>馀杭镂本亡三十篇，而脱句漏字，合三万馀言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1206402_comment'></div>此本传之于东牟王氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1206402_comment'></div>今四明使君，元丰初奉诏修书于资善堂，取大清楼所藏本校定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1206402_comment'></div>元祐壬申，余卧疾京师，喜得此书，每药艾之间手校之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1206402_comment'></div>自秋涉冬，朱黄始就，即为一客挟之而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1206402_comment'></div>后三年见归，而颇有欲得色，余亦心许之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1206402_comment'></div>得官江夏，因募笔工录之，竟以手校本寄欲得者云。<div class='inline' class='label'>按：</span>《吕氏春秋》卷首，元至正嘉兴路儒学刻本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1206402_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_4_183377_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年5月</a>　是年五月,居汴京,有赠友人诗。作品：《赠张之才》<div id='poem_183533' id='poem_sentence_4_183533_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年5月15日</a>　是年春夏,汴京多雨,卧病;五月望日,雨霁天晴,病好赋诗。作品：《夏夜雨晴遣怀》<div id='poem_183679' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183679' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183679?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夏夜雨晴遣怀<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1093年5月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183679")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183679_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183679_0'>① 癸酉岁，京师春夏厌雨，吾居望春门东牛行街，故西枢渤海公之高斋，嘉树清风，殊不知暑湿。时卧病杜门，每把书自适。五月望，雨始收霁，疾亦少间，因赋是诗</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183679'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183679'>积潦被广陌，谁过牛侩翁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183679'>闭关养尪瘵，药石收良工。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183679'>高斋俯嘉樾，疏箔延清风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183679'>左右列图史，披张俄一通。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183679'>从嗤獭祭鱼，聊学蠹书虫。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183679'>坐挹古人语，孰云吾道穷。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183679'>浮生梦境间，不蒂之惊蓬。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183679'>生死犹物化，今昔贤愚同。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183679'>分阴贱垂棘，白日莫再中。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183679'>薄暮纷滓澄，寥寥还太空。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_183679'>为问此何夕，凉蟾生自东。<div id='poem_sentence_10_183679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_183679'>荒哉西园士，联盖追轻鸿。<div id='poem_sentence_11_183679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_183679'>行乐以至斯，不知息微躬。<div id='poem_sentence_12_183679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_183679'>侧聆天鸡鸣，凡耳初破聋。<div id='poem_sentence_13_183679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_183679'>吾从汗漫游，溯景鞭垂虹。<div id='poem_sentence_14_183679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_183679'>濯缨咸池渊，晞发若木<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>丛。<div id='poem_sentence_15_183679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_183679'>亲串不我忘，惠音赤鲩公。<div id='poem_sentence_16_183679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_183679'>长哦赋来归，阅尔世上雄。<div id='poem_sentence_17_183679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_183679'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_183679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年8月</a>　是年八月,在京,有诗。作品：《谢米雍丘元章见过》《秋衣闻雨晨兴偶书》<div id='poem_183503' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183503' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年9月</a>　是年九月,将扶病携家东归山阴,感而赋诗。作品：《寄题栗亭县名嘉亭》<div id='poem_183707' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183707' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183707?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄题栗亭县名嘉亭<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1093年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183707")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183707_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183707_0'>① 邑令赵洋更此新亭名，取杜甫《同谷纪行诗》“栗亭名更嘉”之句。因其亲熊希邈求吾诗。癸酉九月，将扶疾东下，感而为赋</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183707'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183707'>少陵昔避地，幽栖凤皇川。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183707'>始愿获其所，赋诗此终焉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183707'>眷彼美林麓，荫膏腴上田。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183707'>阳坡饶垂珠，阴谷繁玉延。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183707'>长镵勤采斸，服食攀飞仙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183707'>兵祲夺和气，力耕无善年。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183707'>林坰开冰雪，旬浃断庖烟。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183707'>茂宰怆怀古，增崇殊过前。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 磁县（滏阳）

id='poem_sentence_3_183350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183350'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_183350_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183645' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183645' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183645?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故邺<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1078年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183645")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183645_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183645_0'>① 按《邺都记》，汉建安十二年，曹操灭袁氏，始大筑邺。当时京兆、洛阳、南阳、许皆大都，而邺为之长。操子丕代汉，复定都洛阳。此后僭窃更据邺，而未始残破。元魏孝文帝自代南巡，驻跸邺下。久之，以南望枉人山、北接柏人县，非善地，遂去之河南。将行，挂饭罂于城楼上。识者解之，挂饭，悬飧也，岂待玄孙宅此乎。至孝静帝，果为高欢劫，迁都邺。齐五主营建宫室，规模壮丽，远逾前魏。周武平齐，焚撤略尽。及杨坚克尉迥，遂洿潴之，筑京观于葛屦山，徙郡治安阳，邺犹为属邑。熙宁间始废之。戊午九月独游晚归，马上赋</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183645'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183645'>魏武昔恢图，北平谭尚孽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183645'>卜邺筑新都，非徒三狡穴<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集作为三穴）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183645'>将行迁鼎志，遽有分香诀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183645'>落日繐帷空，奠终歌舞阕。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183645'>旋闻瀍洛上，载起苍龙阙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183645'>四叶不归东，苔花驰道绝。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183645'>食槽谶终验，挂饭期先决。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183645'>扰攘百年间，覆车寻此辙<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集作累车寻覆辙）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183645'>山川气象变，朝市繁华歇。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183645'>白露复青芜，茫茫换时节。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_183645'>阴风吹葛屦，燐火走兵血。<div id='poem_sentence_12_183645'>当时陪葬骨，马鬣犹环列。<div id='poem_sentence_12_183645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_183645'>隧碣仆纵横，镌文久残缺。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年9月9日</a>　是年重阳日,酬答友人有诗。作品：《和答郑郎中见寄》<div id='poem_183401' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183401' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_183401_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183401_0'>① 郑，临城人，名渊，字邻几，登进士第，仕至职方郎中。年垂七十，即谢事，居近泜水，自目为泜川逸老。性嗜诗，虽老不废，与余酬唱累数十百篇。既来滏阳，复有诗见寄，因和答之。余诗用它人韵者皆不取，特录此篇，欲见斯人于集中耳。时元丰己未重阳日赋</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183401'><div 庚申七月，客过滏阳，道近时有人观庖人宰三鸡，一雄就缚而鸣不辍，因叹曰：禽鸟将死，知时且鸣，吾安得默默求容于世。因极口肆言，俄抵机阱，几不得免。余感而赋此云</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183712'><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年9月10日</a>　是年九月,在滏阳,有题诗。作品：《题兰陵王碑阴》<div id='poem_183744' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183744' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183744?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题兰陵王碑阴<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1080年9月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183744")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183744_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183744_0'>① 碑载，王名肃，字长恭，北齐文襄之子。按《北史》直书长恭而没其名，盖当时以字行而史失其详尔。王有武略，善抚士，每得一瓜数李，必分甘饵众。金墉之战，免胄先登，推功第一。今《兰陵王曲》即凯歌也。为后主所忌，得疾不治，而卒以鸩薨。碑阴刻王弟延宗一诗，甚哀。墓在滏阳西南十里，道占其东。夏潦所凑，垄已半圮。碑字大兼寸，隶法有古气而不著书人名，文乃卢思道也。庚申九月十日赋</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183744'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183744'>齐室生武贤，兰陵乃颇牧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183744_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183744'>析瓜飨虎士，餍饫<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>比粱肉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183744_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183744'>金墉免胄战，破阵何神速。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183744_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183744'>乐府有遗声，当歌凯旋曲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183744_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183744'>盘宗既不寿，霸祚宜尔促。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183744_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183744'>十代六百年，人间换陵谷。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183744_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183744'>荒途接幽垄，谁复禁樵牧。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183744_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183744'>窆石半攲摧，钩锄断鳌足。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183744_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183744'>苍苔蚀瑑<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作琢）</span>刻，仰睇眩尘目。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183744_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183744'>操翰无愧辞，千言不为辱。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183744_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_183744'>流湍齧马鬣，客土日危蹙。<div id='poem_sentence_10_183744_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_183744'>霪潦并年间，弥漫即川陆。<div id='poem_sentence_11_183744_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_183744'>昔多万两送，今无一抔筑。<div id='poem_sentence_12_183744_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_183744'>人生妄区别，共尽同草木。<div id='poem_sentence_13_183744_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_183744'>何待雍门弹，令君泪盈匊。<div id='poem_sentence_14_183744_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_183744'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_183744_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_183744'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_183744_0'>⑴ 原作尉餍，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_183744_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年9月</a>　是年九月,再游邯郸,有诗。作品：《邯郸郡楼晚望》<div id='poem_183539' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183539' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183539?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邯郸郡楼晚望<span class='inlineComment2'>（庚申九月赋）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1080年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183539'>新凉泻轩槛，草木带秋声。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183539_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183539'>阔水倒岚影，洗磨刀戟明。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183539_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183539'>百虫暮吟动，一鸟归思轻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183539_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183539'>晚律骇徂景，羁怀念劳生。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183539_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183539'>去国亦已久，己年今复庚。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183539'>顾我实荒浪，误抛樵与耕。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183539_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183539'>竹木微径在，奚独古人行。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年9月</a>　是年九月,在滏阳,酬答友人赋诗。作品：《答杜仲观登丛台见寄》<div id='poem_183729' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183729' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_4_183729_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183729'>仕道<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>塞榛芜，低徊避蚖蝮。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183871'>无限悲凉，不胜憔悴，断尽危肠销尽魂。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183871'>方年少，恨浮名误我，乐事输人。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_183871_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

id='poem_content_183412'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183412'>小阁烧香麝煎浓，翠苔庭院绿阴风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183412_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183412_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183412'>西园酒伴无消息，欲寄鱼笺水自东。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183412_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183412'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_183412_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_1_183411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183411'>漫赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作汗）</span>新诗题琬琰，少逢佳客佩兰荪。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1081&endYear=1081')">1081年7月</a>　是年七月,客寓冠氏,游邯郸,与邑令杜俨同赋《丛台歌》诗。<div id='poem_183569' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183569' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183569?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丛台歌<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1081年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183569")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183569_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183569_0'>① 按《邯郸县谱》：丛台，赵武灵王筑，起地三百尺。今故址犹十仞，在县中东北隅。元丰辛酉七月，同邑令濮人杜俨仲观登。杜先有此诗，要余同赋</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183569'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183569'>累土三百尺，流火二千年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183569'>人生物数不相待，摧颓故址秋风前。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183569'>武灵旧垄今安在，秃树无阴困樵采。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183569'>玉箫金镜未销沈，几见耕夫到城卖。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183569'>君不见丛台全盛时，绮罗成市游春晖。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183569'>一从雕辇闭荒草，萧散行云无复归。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183569'>韶<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作招）</span>魂想像风流在<span id='poem_sentence_6_183569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183569'>盘纡棘径撩人衣，禾黍晚成貊貉肥。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183569'>层檐碧瓦碎平地，梦作鸳鸯相伴飞。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183569'>登临吊古将语谁，城郭人民今是非。<div showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183702?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄杜邯郸<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1081年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_sentence_0_183593'>莫问居人溺与逃，破篱敧屋宿渔舠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183593'>中庭老树秋风后，鹳鹤将雏夺鹊巢。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183593'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_183593_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
徐州（彭城）
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年7月</a>　是年七月,自京赴徐,道中赋诗。作品：《晚泊会亭》<div id='poem_183295' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183295' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183295?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晚泊会亭<span class='inlineComment2'>（壬戌七月赋）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1082年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183295")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_183295_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183295'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183295'>后<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>日符离复舍舟，马蹄尘土入徐州。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183295'>祇应明月曾相识，伴我时登燕子楼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183295'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_183295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_183295'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_183295_0'>⑴ 原作复，据清抄本、四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_183295_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年7月</a>　是年七月,自京赴徐,夜行邹县道中作诗。作品：《夜行邹县道中遇雨作》<div id='poem_183638' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183638' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183638?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夜行邹县道中遇雨作<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1082年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183638")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183638_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183638_0'>① 乙丑八月被外计檄自徐趋郓，道中赋</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183638'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183638'>昨日秋遂分，村村敛禾黍。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183638'>半夜宿田人，相嘑<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：去）</span>深陂雨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183638'>骎骎马上客，厌浥投何所。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183638'>暮发邹子城，朝期饭东鲁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183638'>据鞍思假寐，颠坠惭不武。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183638'>俯畏道旁石，颓然如伏虎。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183638'>远惊荞麦华，白水漫洲渚。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183638'>安能叱吾驭，亲闱寄西楚。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183638'>念昔卧苏门，夙兴犹及午。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183638'>岂谓从一官，羁离遽如许。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_183638'>归欤惜迟暮，幽愫将谁语。<div id='poem_sentence_10_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_183638'>赖尔草根虫，助我长吟苦。<div id='poem_sentence_11_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_183638'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_183638_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年8月</a>　是年八月,在徐,怀故人杜俨有诗。作品：《寄杜仲观》<div id='poem_183701' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183701' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183701?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄杜仲观<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1082年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183701")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183701_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183701_0'>① 辛酉二月，余罢官滏阳，访仲观于邯郸。属雨后晴和，城邑人已衣袷。既登丛台，风色凄紧，尚如隆冬。时台下有佛祠，庭中得断碑，乃蔡有邻书严挺之《丛台怀古赋》也，因请仲观树之壁间。佛祠西去二三里，有王氏园，偶诸俳倡将祀神者，因置酒按之。邑人丘岩起次说与焉，明日相别。是冬，仲观亦受代，复调南康船官。壬戌八月，余至彭城，登高有怀，因赋此以寄</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183701'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183701'>中春雨收霁，与子登丛台。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183701'>形胜宛然在，太行西北来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183701'>无情百尺土，千载未摧颓。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183701'>四顾发悲啸，凄风振颐颏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183701'>淩高气象变，似不容徘徊。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183701'>下出破禅刹，断碑生紫苔。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183701'>严公赋怀古，复使后人哀。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183701'>西寻王氏园，一径趋城隈。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183701'>老竹未萌笋，繁花如雪开。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183701'>惠然丘<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集作美）</span>少年，逸躅欣攀陪。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_183701'>小榭罗宴豆，开帘按俳诙。<div id='poem_sentence_10_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_183701'>招呼缈缥<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作缥缈）</span>人，晚镜<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>催妆梅。<div id='poem_sentence_11_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_183701'>水调唱金缕，云罍浮玉醅。<div id='poem_sentence_12_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_183701'>倾觞敢惜醉，忘著接䍦回。<div id='poem_sentence_13_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_183701'>明日遂分首<span class='inlineComment2'>（清抄本、四库本作手）</span>，旧游安在哉。<div id='poem_sentence_14_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_183701'>我为东徐官，客鬓栖尘埃。<div id='poem_sentence_15_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_183701'>君调南康吏，江山役清才。<div id='poem_sentence_16_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_183701'>西风吹去雁，尺纸为君裁。<div id='poem_sentence_17_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_183701'>我已困摧辱，壮心如湿灰。<div id='poem_sentence_18_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_183701'>行将隐名姓，采药孙登嵬<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注；共城山名。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_19_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_183701'>异日傥相过，衡门剪蒿莱。<div id='poem_sentence_20_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_183701'></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_183701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_183701'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_11_183701_0'>⑴ 清抄本、四库本作钟</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_183701_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年8月</a>　是年八月,在徐,有登楼怀贬黄州故人苏子瞻诗。作品：《登黄楼有怀苏眉山》<div id='poem_183727' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183727' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183727?labeling=true' target='_blank'>登黄楼有怀苏眉山<span class='inlineComment2'>（时公谪居黄冈。壬戌八月彭城作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1082年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183727")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183727_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183727'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183727'>登黄楼，望黄州，黄州望不见，楼下水东流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183727'>水流何可留，浮云更悠悠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183727'>伤心泽畔客，憔悴楚兰秋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_183727_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年</a>　是年八月,在徐州,有诗。作品：《游云龙张氏山居》《秋怀二首》<div id='poem_183721' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183721' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183721?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游云龙张氏山居<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1082年8月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183721")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183721_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183721_0'>① 云龙山距彭城郭南三里，郡人张天骥圣涂筑亭于西麓。元丰初，郡守眉山苏公屡登燕于此亭下，畜二鹤，因以放鹤名亭，复为之记。亭下有小屋曰苏斋，壁间榜眉山所留二诗及画大枯株，亦公醉笔也。亭上一径至山腹，有石如砻治者，公复题三十许字，记戊午仲冬雪后与二三子携惠山泉、烹凤团此岩下，张即镵之。壬戌秋，余初至徐，张惠然见临，继相招为（四库本作与）山中游。八月晦日，遂往。暮归，马上赋此诗</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183721'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183721'>昔闻张逸民，卜筑云龙山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183721'>东望结遐想，喜得彭城官。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183721'>一语定襟契，宛如平生欢。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183721'>招携属休沐，投此萝薜间。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183721'>女仆候门巷，青袿双翠鬟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183721'>苏斋轩户明，饼火焚椒兰。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183721'>宝墨鬼神护，清诗冰玉寒。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183721'>森然拱檐霤，架石排琅玕。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183721'>东趋放鹤亭，磴道披茅菅。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183721'>指顾百村落，炊烟林莽间。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_183721'>日脚洒平陆，两山如断环。<div id='poem_sentence_10_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_183721'>凄风振晚叶，坐怯衣裘单。<div id='poem_sentence_11_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_183721'>引领紫霄极，飘飖如可干。<div id='poem_sentence_12_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_183721'>缅怀眉山公，五马来游盘。<div id='poem_sentence_13_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_183721'>酣兴走颠笔，苍崖即镵刊。<div id='poem_sentence_14_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_183721'>午年仲冬月，雪野云弥漫。<div id='poem_sentence_15_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_183721'>扫石坐舒啸，惠泉烹凤团。<div id='poem_sentence_16_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_183721'>当时诧盛集，千古陋逵安。<div id='poem_sentence_17_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_183721'>俛仰迹遂陈，斯人久泥蟠。<div id='poem_sentence_18_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_183721'>我来后千日，逸躅何由攀。<div id='poem_sentence_19_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_183721'>遇胜不能赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集作仰怀胜事往）</span>，俯寻<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集作遵）</span>尘路还。<div id='poem_sentence_20_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_183721'>山英移未勒<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集作能不辱）</span>，时款白云关。<div id='poem_sentence_21_183721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_183721'></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_183721_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183420' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183420' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183420?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋怀二首<span class='inlineComment2'>（壬戌九月彭城赋）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1082年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183420")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183420_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183420'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183420'>室迩人尚远，况乎千里间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183420_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183420'>岂徒道路长，重水复重山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183420_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183420'>清霜老芳物，嘉树不堪攀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183420_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183420'>欲寄陇头信，春风殊未还。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183420_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183420'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_183420_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183648' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183648' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183648?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1082年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183648_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183648'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183648'>萧萧庭木落，格格鸡声恶。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183648'>荒檐日影斜，饥猫捕黄雀。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183648_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年9月</a>　是年九月,在徐州,有诗。作品：《题彭城张氏放鹤亭》《答陈传道》<div id='poem_183524' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183524' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183524?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题彭城张氏放鹤亭<sup class='reference class='inlineComment2'>（小集作曾）</span>卜筑如相待，今遂登临是不期。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183524_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183524'>万顷白云山缺处，一庭黄叶雨来时。<div id='poem_content_183501'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183501'>吾家季真登大蓬，我为斗筲来宝丰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183501_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_183328_0'>① 壬戌彭城赋（仅存诗题，缺诗文，据清抄本、四库本补）</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183328'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183328'>当时节物此山川，倦客登临独惘然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183328'>戏马台荒年自久，射蛇公去事空传。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年9月9日</a>　是年重九,在徐州,有词,徐州词可考者止此。作品：《玉京秋》（陇首霜晴）<div id='poem_183828' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183828' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183828'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183828'>陇首霜晴，泗滨云晚，乍摇落。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183828_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183828'>废榭苍苔，破台荒草，西楚霸图冥漠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183828_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183828'>记登临事，九日胜游，千载如昨。<div href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年9月10日</a>　是年九月,在徐州,登燕子楼,与僚友分韵赋诗。作品：《燕子楼》<div id='poem_183760' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183760' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183760?labeling=true' target='_blank'>燕子楼<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1082年9月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183760")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183760_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183760_0'>① 唐徐牧张建封晚得姬人盼盼，宠嬖之，为起燕子楼于使宅北城上，以处焉。后更兵火，楼不复存。天圣中，故相濮阳李公出守彭城，复楼于故址。壬戌重九后一日，余与二三僚友置酒楼上，分韵赋诗，偶得如字。而侍酒官妓亦有名盼盼者，盖窃希唐人，因为见于卒章</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183760'><div 彭城郡城之东南隅，提点刑狱官废廨也。熙宁末，魏郡李公持节来此，构亭城隅之上，郡太守眉山苏公命名曰快哉亭。下有爽垲数十步，即唐人薛能阳春亭故址也。癸亥六月始登此亭，因赋是诗</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183596'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_515626_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_515626'>未应白发饶新贵，任使黄华笑独醒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_515626_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_515626'>异日肯寻鸡黍约，太行长绕故园青。<div id='poem_sentence_3_515626_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_515626'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_515626_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年10月</a>　是年十月，在徐州,有诗怀苏轼。作品：《题彭城南台寺苏眉山诗刻后》<div id='poem_183531' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183531' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183531?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题彭城南台寺苏眉山诗刻后<sup class='reference "poem_title_183531")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_183531_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183531_0'>① 癸亥十月，徐之走卒还自京师，误传苏黄州被召。南台寺公旧题数诗，先摹刻诸石，因赋此书其左</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183531'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183531'>秋风几度老江蓠，鼎水眉峰隔梦思。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183531_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183531'>下走误传宣室召，上前谁进子虚辞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183531_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183531'>东坡麋鹿同三径，西掖鹓鸾占一枝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183531_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183531'>独有野僧违一<span class='inlineComment2'>（清抄本作末）</span>俗，翠珉新勒旧题诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183531_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183531'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_183531_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年12月10日</a>　是年十二月十日,在徐州,与友人登飞鸿亭赋诗。作品：《飞鸿亭》<div id='poem_183556' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183556' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183556?labeling=true' target='_blank'>飞鸿亭<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年12月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183556")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183556_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183556_0'>① 彭城南禅佛祠，据戏马台之麓，有岩山出其上方，广倍寻，可立柱石。癸亥秋九月，太守河南王公说命僧起亭冠焉。亭成，置酒以落之，而未得嘉名以称也。时天晴木落，旅雁南下，复有声琴于坐者，公偶诵嵇叔夜“目送归鸿，手拊五弦”之句，因以飞鸿榜之。是冬十二月十日，复与李昭玘成父、杨中立同登，因赋是诗</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183556'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183556'>禅林跨山胁，飞构凿崚嶒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183556'>千里寄双睫，百忧消一登。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183556'>斯游属公暇，晓日东南升。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183556'>霜野明练甲，云阴垂海鹏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183556'>东州地阳暖，腊月川无冰。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183556'>大艑<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作船）</span>出洪口，突去如骞腾。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183556'>趺<sup class='reference id='poem_sentence_7_183556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183556'>矫首发长啸，清风鼓尘膺。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183556'>寥寥紫虚路，鸿雁正凭凌。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_183556'>仿像中散公，俯手朱丝绳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183612'>宿衾熏萏菡，朝镜拂漪涟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183612'>津润销金笔，香依扑粉绵。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183612'>鹦鹉殷勤语，旃檀委曲烟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183612'>鲛绡乾玉箸，鱼钥限金莲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183612'>朱门长窅窅，白马自翩翩。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_183576' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183576' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183576?labeling=true' target='_blank'>田园乐<sup class='reference 甲子八月，与彭城诗社诸君会南台佛祠，望田亩秋成，农有喜色。诵王摩诘（原作诰，据清抄本、四库本改）b《田园乐》，因分韵拟之，余得村字</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183576'><div class='poemSentence' class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183393_0'>① 乙丑正月晦日，与余乡段询慎从、李成父、寇元弼步出彭城之上洪门，泛舟访张谋父于白云庄。晚归皆被酒，段集古人句成二首示同游，余因走笔和之以送谋父。后旬馀，慎从感疾物故，张复出是诗，使人泣叹弥日</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年8月</a>　是年秋,在徐,有诗。作品：《和张谋父游石佛山观魏太武书》<div id='poem_183627' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183627' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183627?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和张谋父游石佛山观魏太武书<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183627")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183627_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183627_0'>① 按《南北史》、《彭城图经》：魏太平真君十一年，太武南侵至瓜步，筑宫驻跸，声欲渡江。宋人患之，遣使请婚，馈百牢以犒师。明年春，旋师渡淮，复留连徐方再旬，始北去。今彭城南五里，因山镵佛，高十许丈。东北百步有大磐石，敧枕小溪，划然四字曰阿弥陀佛，皆径尺馀，特陀佛两字为逸笔结之，其长倍寻，下落溪中。盖当时太武以铁箠画是字，非刊刻也。乙丑秋，张谋父摹墨本见惠，兼赋一诗，要余属和焉</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183627'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183627'>中夏昔屯否，代邦天所开。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183627_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183627_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183627'>云旗即归路，览胜此裴徊。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183627_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_183627'>茫茫六百年，风雨生莓苔。<div id='poem_sentence_10_183627_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_183627'>伟迹寖销泯，威灵安在哉。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年10月</a>　是年十月,在徐,应友人陈传道之请,为其双沟官舍濒水之北轩题诗。作品：《题渊明轩》<div id='poem_183530' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183530' class='poemTitle id='poem_title_183530_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183530_0'>① 陈传道葺双沟官舍濒水之北轩，索名于我，因命曰渊明轩。陈即日去职，余高斯人，为赋是诗，寄题轩上。乙丑十月彭城作</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183530'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183530'>渊明新<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作轩）</span>榜揭门眉，夫子高情俗不知。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183530'>卧来不浅羲皇兴，归去何惭乡里儿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183530_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183530'>窗破檐倾从此始，祇应风月解相思。<div id='poem_content_183545'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183545'>人生七十稀，行年今已半。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183545_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183545'>名姓系西班，星霜亟徂换。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183545_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183545'>未筑黄金台，长歌白石烂。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183545_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183545'>岂无同心契，相望眇云汉。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183545_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183545'>每虞狂<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>飙至，摧折涧底干。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183545_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183545'>异日偶班输，抱柯徒永叹。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183545_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_183545'></div><div id='poem_note_183545_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: 郓城

id='poem_title_183638_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183638_0'>① 乙丑八月被外计檄自徐趋郓，道中赋</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183638'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183638'>昨日秋遂分，村村敛禾黍。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183638'>半夜宿田人，相嘑<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：去）</span>深陂雨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183638'>骎骎马上客，厌浥投何所。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183638'>暮发邹子城，朝期饭东鲁。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183638'>安能叱吾驭，亲闱寄西楚。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183638'>念昔卧苏门，夙兴犹及午。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183638'>岂谓从一官，羁离遽如许。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_183638'>归欤惜迟暮，幽愫将谁语。<div id='poem_sentence_10_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_183638'>赖尔草根虫，助我长吟苦。<div id='poem_sentence_11_183638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_183638'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_183638_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>是年八月,被外计檄召,徐郓往返途中有诗。作品：《行路难》<div id='poem_183589' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_2_183589'>驱车何所投，却顾归路长。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183589'>挟辕两羸牸，犯此豺<span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年10月</a>　是年十月,东归过雍丘,留别米芾赋诗。作品：《留别米雍丘》二首。<div id='poem_183456' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183456' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183456")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_183456_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183456_0'>① 米辨博有才具，著《山林集》数十卷，为人知者特水淫、书学而已。清狂多忤，尝上章援余祠史之请，不报辄已，因以激之。癸酉十月雍丘赋</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183456'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183456'>明釭通夜语，累块写胸中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183456'>水癖推刘令，书名浼鲁公。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183456'>忌猜悲廪鼠，逐热贱云鸿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183456'>不乏佳山水，东南著两翁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183456'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_183456_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183457' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183457' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183457?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1093年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_183457_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183457'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183457'>好住楚公子，山林何处逢。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183457'>官身须自乞，俗眼可相容。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183457'>叔夜懒犹锻，伯鸾佣且舂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183457'>多惭方禄隐，尔汝傲吴侬。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183457'></div><div -----title
灵璧（零壁）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3b623834a90c40d0a49d9377f1de9d17_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3b623834a90c40d0a49d9377f1de9d17");'><span id='3b623834a90c40d0a49d9377f1de9d17_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年</a>，37岁</div><div id='3b623834a90c40d0a49d9377f1de9d17' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年2月</a>　是年二月,舟行次灵璧,游园有诗。作品：《游灵璧兰皋园》<div id='poem_183723' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183723' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183723?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游灵壁兰皋园<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183723")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183723_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183723_0'>① 集贤张校理治此园以奉亲，因名兰皋。戊辰二月，余舟行次灵壁，访张氏子硕，于园中诸亭壁间，得故人东莱寇元弼三四诗，因继题十八韵，兼简元弼</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183723'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183723'>集仙昔荣养，卜筑循兰陔。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183723'>深径万株合，清池百亩开。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183723'>飞梁荫菡萏，攒栋跨崔嵬。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183723'>淮海斸红药，潇湘移翠栽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183723'>岱松佩萝茑，海石糊莓苔。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183723'>车马远惊聒，鱼鸟忘嫌猜。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183723'>病客倦舟楫，寻春此裴徊。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183723'>闰年物候迟，前日已闻雷。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183723'>薄景未晞雪，东风新破梅。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183723'>主人京洛旧，杖屦容参陪。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_183723'>指我艮隅地，方营秋月台。<div id='poem_sentence_10_183723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_183723'>眼明壁间字，醉墨题东莱。<div id='poem_sentence_11_183723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_183723'>短句颇清绝，早推能赋才。<div id='poem_sentence_12_183723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_183723'>殷勤卷白苧，为尔拂尘埃。<div id='poem_sentence_13_183723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_183723'>安得一携手，更倾林下杯。<div id='poem_sentence_14_183723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_183723'>酒阑话平昔，岂复顾形骸。<div id='poem_sentence_15_183723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_183723'>行役浸相远，人生信悠哉。<div id='poem_sentence_16_183723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_183723'>薄暮重回首，长哦归去来。<div id='poem_sentence_17_183723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_183723'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_183723_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
天长
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bc186c1899414d249c85da10995e9e9a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bc186c1899414d249c85da10995e9e9a");'><span id='bc186c1899414d249c85da10995e9e9a_link' id='poem_sentence_5_183816'>泪洒春风，春风谁复管。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_183816_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183830' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183830' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_183830'>人自起、翠衾寒梦，夜来风恶。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183830_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183830'>肠断残红和泪落。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183830_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183830'>半随经雨飘池角。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183830_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183830'>记采兰、携手曲江游，年时约。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183830_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183830'>芳物大，都如昨。<div 南京（江宁）
-----detail

id='poem_sentence_0_183488_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183488'>江山月照六朝梦，桃李风吹三月春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183488_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 在城之西南，盖生公讲堂故址也。南即石子冈，登览尽江南之胜。戊辰三月，舟次金陵，与同行李延永游，西望石迹戍，才如数里之许耳</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183725'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183725'>迢迢朱雀航，飞盖共淩越。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183725'>东风石子冈，芳草微径绝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_content_183355'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183355'>六代风流不可寻，石头胜槩古犹今。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183499'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183499'>声迹相闻忽此逢，杖藜萧散一相从。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183763' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183763?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠僧孚<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span id='poem_sentence_5_183763_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183763'>扁舟三月溯长川，故人投谒俄童颠。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183763_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年4月7日</a>　是年四月,宿历阳西南九十里之法惠寺题诗。作品：《宿法惠寺》<div id='poem_183697' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183697' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183697?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宿法惠寺<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年4月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183697")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183697_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183697_0'>① 在历阳西南九十里。戊辰四月七日，沿事至顺天里，越斗岘山、冷泉涧，薄晚投宿此寺。寺三隅面山而豁其西北，竹树邃密，如不与人境相接。庭中有泉如轮，清洌而甘。跨山起小阁，榜曰馀翠。登望旷快，因赋是诗题其上</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183697'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183697'>重门壮且深，老柏森然行。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183697'>佛子出延客，投鞭步长廊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183697'>中庭汲新泉，一饮生清凉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183565'>时平一登望，江山互襟带。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183565'>想像文献公，清风宛如在。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183565'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_183565_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183563' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183563' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183563?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>当利港<sup class='reference class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183563_0'>① 县东二里，下通大江。按县谱，晋王浚征吴，乘便风趋石头，王浑招之不顾，即此地。此（诗题及注三十二字原缺，仅存“诗当在遏胡城之前”八字，据清抄本、四库本补）诗当在遏胡城之前</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183563'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183563'>龙骧乘上游，锐气吞敌境。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183563'>风便趋吴京，收功在俄顷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183563'>平生负雄图，晚岁方获骋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183563'>何必传鼎彝，江山与之永。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href='/Writing/183564?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span>天门山<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1089年5月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183564_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183564_0'>① 县东南五十里，江导两山之间，殊湍悍。按县谱，宋孝武尝驻跸此山上阅水军发，因建二石阙以誇武功，今遗迹在焉</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183564'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183564'>天门束箭流，北注据牛弩<span id='poem_sentence_2_183560'>尘纷晦遗像，粉绘才可睹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183560'>拜奠愧无言，长哦君乐府。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183559_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183561' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183561' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183561?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span>平痾汤<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1089年5月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183561_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183561_0'>① 县西北四十里。按县谱，汤泉下伏丹砂，浴之能愈疾，故有平痾之名。即刘梦得《历阳记》所谓沸井者也</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183561'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183561'>文础护清漪，炯若涵冰玉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年6月</a>　是年六月,在历阳,追忆昔年游览金陵三山有诗。作品：《三山》<div id='poem_183546' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183546' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183546?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三山<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1089年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183546")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183546_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183546_0'>① 在金陵西南百里，崛起大江之中。昔王龙骧顺流鼓棹，径造三山；谢玄晖登三山望京邑，皆此地也。戊辰三月，始游金陵，置酒于凤皇台，引望此山，如落天外，雅符太白诗中语。既渡江，至石迹戍，门适与山对。己巳六月赋是诗</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183546'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183546'>南朝凤皇台，置酒昔高会。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183546'>酒酣望三山，宛在青天外。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183546'>长哦谪仙吟，如啖鲸鲵鲙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183546'>明日信东风，孤帆出其背。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183546'>荒戍接江濆，开门适相对。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183546'>鼎足跱长川，不为舟楫碍。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183546'>雨旸云吞吐，早晏潮进退。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183546'>万古免浮沈，曾微抃鳌戴。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183546'>伊余厌尘坌，闭目何可奈。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183546'>爽气豁襟灵，山乎吾有赖。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_183546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_183546'>他时挂武冠，刀剑行且卖。<div id='poem_sentence_14_183546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年7月</a>　是年七月,在历阳,有诗。作品：《乌江东乡往还马上作》二首。<div id='poem_183336' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183336' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='inlineComment2'>（小集作明）</span>月入牖窥曲房，候虫刺促鸣我床。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183553'>离忧欻来煎人肠，夜如何其夜何长。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183553'>绿琴在荐兮，拟楚奏之沈<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集作沅）</span>湘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183553'>朱弦湿露兮，声戾指而不扬。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183553'>屏琴浩歌兮，屑涕泗之浪浪。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183553'>我有所思兮，在河之阳。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183553'>僾而不见兮，衷<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>难弭忘。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183553'>騄骥腾跃兮，鸿鹄翱翔。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183553'>明珰玉案兮，尔不我将。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_183553'>缄诚结惠兮，久莫汝偿。<div id='poem_sentence_10_183553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_183553'>永如牛女兮，南北相望。<div id='poem_sentence_11_183553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_183553'>昔燕处兮，灵芸之堂。<div id='poem_sentence_12_183553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_183553'>纫兰为佩兮，集芰为裳。<div id='poem_sentence_14_183553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_183553'>兰萎芰裂兮，恐被服之不芳。<div id='poem_sentence_15_183553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 高邮

id='poem_note_183466'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_183466_0'>⑴ 清抄本、四库本作路</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_183466_comment'></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>是年十二月,东归,途经高邮,留别友人有诗。作品：《留别王景通二首》<div id='poem_183454' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183454' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183454?labeling=true' 泗县（盱眙）

class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183740'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183740'>君希谢太傅，筑室卧东山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183740_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' target='_blank'>题海陵寓舍四首<span class='inlineComment2'>（甲戌闰月赋）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年4月闰月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_sentence_0_183525_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183525'>暮凉百燕抵突雨，昼静一蝉饕餮风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183525_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183525'>隐几敢希南郭久，移文方诮北山空。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183525_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183525'>森然槐柳相差地<span id='poem_sentence_4_183525_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183755' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183755' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183755?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_2_183755'>辗转犹憎<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作增）</span>夏夜久，支离何堪春病馀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183755_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183655'>卞山之下苕溪滨，一洗长安肥马尘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183655'>君不见昔人负米长勤捧檄喜，敢论州县徒劳耳。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183655'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_183655_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年6月</a>　是年六月,于海陵,有送别诗。作品：《送海陵周太守邠受代还朝》<div id='poem_183667' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183667' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183667?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送海陵周太守邠受代还朝<sup class='reference 周字开（原作闬，据清抄本改）祖，尝宰管城有声。甲戌六月赋</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183667'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183667'>汤汤水东流，奈何载此西行舟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183667'>紞如五鼓鸣城头，使君去矣不可留。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183667'>不关外户息吠犬，悉把钩锄谁带牛。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183667'>雨旸不违祷，舄卤数倍收。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183667'>吏却一钱贿，狱无五木囚。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183667'>黄堂坐啸有馀暇，八咏新诗追隐侯。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_183667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_183667'>问君何以治海陵，但陈圣主之德臣何能，狂生有意水衡丞。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_183667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_183667'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_183667_0'>⑴ 原作哦，据清抄本、四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_183667_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　是年夏旱,海陵苏氏所居南有小池畜双鹤,饥立庭除,主人莫恤,感而赋诗。作品：《老鹤叹》<div id='poem_183586' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183586' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183586?labeling=true' target='_blank'>老鹤叹<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183586")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183586_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183586_0'>① 海陵苏氏，即居之南凿小池以畜双鹤。甲戌夏旱，池涸如陆，是鹤饥立庭除间，主人莫恤也，因赋诗以靳（清抄本、四库本作叹）之</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183586'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183586'>华表华表归来乎，出无车<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本下有兮字）</span>，食无鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183586'>懿公之遇难再图，卑栖剩啄同群雏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183586'>谁谓<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>嵇氏子不孤，强颜市井交屠沽，巨源密启亦已疏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183586'>呜呼，卫侯既不可作，道林今也则无。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183586'>露鸣风舞何区区，夙夜供君耳目娱。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183586'>西山二子饥相似，南国三闾放不如。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183586'>端虑盘飧怀异味，并随焦尾付庖厨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_183586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_183586'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_183586_0'>⑴ 原作谓谁，据清抄本、四库本乙</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_183586_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　是年七月,在海陵,有诗。作品：《送僧还嘉兴》<span class='inlineComment2'>（王梦隐张家顺《庆湖遗老诗集校注》,河南大学出版社2008年版，第41页，题作《送僧云还吴兴》,两诗应为同一首诗。）</span>《许永席上赋》<div id='poem_183671' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183671' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183671?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送僧云还吴兴<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183671")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183671_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183671_0'>① 云喜作小诗，稍不俗。甲戌（原作戊，据清抄本、四库本改）七月海陵赋</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183671'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183671'>吴兴道人美风度，月下沧浪翘白鹭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183671'>昼公诗律尚能传，间有赤乌黄耳句。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183671'>海角相逢一笑新，怀归不待白蘋春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183671'>寄声故国群儿辈，潦倒尘埃贺季真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183671'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_183671_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183374' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183374' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183374?labeling=true' target='_blank'>许永席上赋<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年7月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183374")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_183374_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183374_0'>① 许字子长，家酿甚美，名十八仙。时余抱病节酒，而欢亦同之。甲戌中元日海陵赋</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183374'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183374'>流浪江湖跨两年，西风犹驻木兰船。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183374'>可人方外二三子，与尔樽中十八仙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183374'>处士<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作女）</span>妄同公子议，曲生未减索郎贤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183374'>自怜衰病方轰饮，也在刘家幕下天。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183374'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_183374_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
芜湖
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='05c0a65eaf7c427ca77c9ef3afa69694_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("05c0a65eaf7c427ca77c9ef3afa69694");'><span id='05c0a65eaf7c427ca77c9ef3afa69694_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>，45岁</div><div id='05c0a65eaf7c427ca77c9ef3afa69694' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年4月</a>　是年四月,赴江夏宝泉监任,过芜湖游王敦城,有诗。作品：《芜湖王敦城下作》<div id='poem_183387' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183387' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183387?labeling=true' target='_blank'>芜湖王敦城下作<span class='inlineComment2'>（丙子四月赋）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183387")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_183387_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183387'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183387'>斗立孤城日四围，贼奴曾未慑天威。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183387'>风生虎帐豺声厉，尘犯龙颜鱼服归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183387'>首揭大航遗臭在，歌流乐府旧音非。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183387'>当时不慕桓文举，草满中原胡马肥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183387'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_183387_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
潜山（宿松）
-----detail

九江

id='poem_sentence_6_183669'>渊明为酒接休元，我每移书谢州牧。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183669'>渊明纸笔课儿曹，我子长歌紫芝曲。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183669'>萧闲门户十三年，尚畏尘缘生处熟。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183669'>行将卜隐包家山，誓与苍生鍊大还。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183669_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_183669'>愿君门外诛榛菅，来者勿拒容跻攀。<div -----title
武汉（汉阳）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='09241663f18145809c5f4d50ff00f79d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("09241663f18145809c5f4d50ff00f79d");'><span id='09241663f18145809c5f4d50ff00f79d_link'
