href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年5月</a>　是年五月,抵汉阳,应友人之求赋诗。作品：《寄题浔阳周氏濂溪草堂》<div id='poem_183706' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183706' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183706?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄题浔阳周氏濂溪草堂<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183706")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183706_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183706_0'>① 周本江华人，名敦颐，字茂叔，仕至尚书郎，累使岭表。中年投节，退居湓城之南溪上，因名濂溪以自况。二子，寿字元翁，焘字次元，相踵第进士。丙子五月，余舣舟汉阳，始与元翁相际，求余赋此诗</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183706'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183706'>濂溪之水清，未足濯公缨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183706'>平生抱苦节，成就此溪名。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183706'>长啸置符传，孤云归思轻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183706'>溪头四壁居，溪下百亩耕。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183706'>量汲奉晨盥，课樵共夕烹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183706'>希逢杖屦游，但听弦歌声。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183706'>为客剪<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集作开）</span>三径，传家通<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集作惟）</span>一经。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183706'>双珠交照乘，合璧倍<span class='inlineComment2'>（小集作价）</span>连城。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183706'>被褐<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>有馀乐，问缣无隐情。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183706'>桂林两枝秀，借尔俗眼荣<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作明）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_183706'>昔仰名父子，今推难弟兄。<div id='poem_sentence_10_183706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_183706'>不应文范裔，遽谓公惭卿。<div id='poem_sentence_11_183706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_183706'>如袭带砺封，毋为权利倾。<div id='poem_sentence_12_183706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_183706'>地实寝丘比，有力安得并。<div id='poem_sentence_13_183706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_183706'>勒诗高岸石，敢告后代生。<div id='poem_sentence_14_183706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_183706'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_183706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_183706'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_8_183706_0'>⑴ 原作褐被，据清抄本、四库本乙</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_183706_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年5月</a>　是年五月,抵汉阳,游郎官湖,有诗。作品：《郎官湖》<div id='poem_183540' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183540' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183540?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郎官湖<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183540")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_183540_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183540_0'>① 按李白诗序云，乾元岁流夜郎，遇故人尚书郎张谓使夏口，沔州杜太守、汉阳王令觞（原作触，据清抄本、四库本改）于江城之南湖。张公四望超然，请白标之嘉名，白因号之郎官湖，席上文士辅翼（清抄本作翌）岑靖以为知言。今所谓郎官湖者，占郡城之北，束于两山间，纵广百许步，固不足四望而超然也，已知其非是。且郡南濒江之人持南唐时地券，尚指郎官湖为邻。盖湖为江水所并，而去城里馀犹有洲渚隐然未泯，乃湖之故防也。余丙子五月舟次沔阳，求访遗老，始得其详，因赋此诗志之</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183540'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183540'>当年贤守令，载酒沔南游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183540'>凉月呈新霁，明湖涵素秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183540'>郎官夏口使，仙客夜郎囚。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183540'>促膝青螭舫，连觞紫绮裘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183540'>高驩随雨散，馀躅想风流。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183540'>芳草失青履，沧波浮白鸥。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183540'>江吞百顷尽，石刻一篇留。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183540'>宜有沈碑者，前怀陵谷忧。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183540'></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年7月</a>　是年七月,抱病汉阳,有诗。作品：《送周寿元翁西上》<div id='poem_183662' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183662' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_4_183327_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_1_183365'>沧浪难为俗子唱，络纬漫催贫女工。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183365'>风月少容休吏役，烟波长与济途穷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183365'>功成身退非吾事，犹办扁舟东复东。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183365'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_183365_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183583' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183583' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_0_183583_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183583'>幽虫切切竟何道，羁燕匆匆将安之。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183583_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183583'>洛下微吟聊拥鼻，西山爽气为支颐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183583_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183583'>肯将翰墨悲流落，寄语三闾彼一时。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183583_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183583'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_183583_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183366' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183366' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183366?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span id='poem_sentence_1_183366_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183366'>千年陈迹祇今日，万里故园犹个中。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183366_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183366_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183268' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183268' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183268?labeling=true' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183268'>记得广陵城里市，董源横障卖千金。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183268'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_183268_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183341' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183341' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183341?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_2_183341_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183341'>销磨髀肉亦何事，竟作子阳同井蛙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183341_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183341'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_183341_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183715' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183715' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183715?labeling=true' target='_blank'>黄鹤楼<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183715")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183715_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183715_0'>① 在鄂州使宅之西南隅，唐阎伯程记云：《图经》载费祎登仙，尝驾黄鹤返憩于此，遂以名楼焉。并见于《神仙传》与《述异记》。按《蜀（原作属，据清抄本、四库本改）书》传，本江夏鄳人也，为刺客郭循所害，岂道家所谓兵解者欤？丙子九月，始登此楼，因赋</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183715'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183715'>登真者谁子，昔有费公祎<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作讳，据清抄本、四库本改）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183715'>白日玉书下，青天驾鹤飞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183715'>此地少留憩，神标怅依依。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183715'>振裾谢尘浊，与尔方远违。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183715'>层楼宠陈迹，江山长四围。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183715'>登临美商素，雨气薄西晖。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183715'>水落州觜嫩，风豪帆背肥。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183715'>飘然起遐想，琳馆閟岩扉。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183715'>明月识悠阔，白云疑是非。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183715'>金桃未遽熟，薤露虞先晞。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_183715'>高树两华表，长招羽驾归。<div id='poem_sentence_10_183715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_183715'>灵瓢五色剂，定与遗民挥。<div id='poem_sentence_11_183715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_183715'>自顾乏<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作非）</span>仙质，延生犹可希。<div id='poem_sentence_12_183715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_183715'>刀圭傥不吝，如饱首阳饥。<div id='poem_sentence_13_183715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_183715'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_183715_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183764' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183764' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183764?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鹦鹉洲<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183764")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183764_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183764_0'>① 在鄂渚南浦上。按《图经》云，因祢衡赋鹦鹉于此洲，遂得名。后黄祖杀衡，投尸此洲下，胡曾诗“祢衡珠翠逐江流”是也。丙子九月赋</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183764'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183764'>鹦鹉陇下鸟，能语奇羽毛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183764'>罗罻巧相致，雕笼关鐍牢。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183764'>长怀故园树，烟雨落空巢。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183764'>万里迁泽国，舟舆□□劳。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183764'>正平托物赋，健笔不停操。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183764'>千载访陈躅，晴沙葭菼高。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183764'>珍禽不复见，慨想若人豪。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183764'>处士起河朔，英风拔时髦。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183764'>文章俪坟诰，俛就犹诗骚。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183764'>儿汝命杨孔，奴兵视刘曹。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_183764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_183764'>非无择木智，天下方滔滔。<div id='poem_sentence_12_183764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_note_183708_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年10月</a>　是年十月,在江夏,有诗。作品：《寄别秦观少游》《寄汉阳赵尉沔》《怀寄周元翁》十首。《题武昌郑判官直节亭》<div id='poem_183471' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183471' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183471?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄别秦观少游<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", id='poem_title_183471_0'>① 秦南迁桂阳，舟过沔上，隔江不及见，因寄是诗。余三为钱官。丙子十月江夏赋</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183471'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183471'>沔阳湖上小留连，疑是前时李谪仙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183471_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183471'>流向夜郎才半道，径<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>还江夏乐当年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183471_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183471'>个侬生以才为累，阿堵官于老有缘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183471_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183471'>待得公归吾亦罢，春风先办两渔船。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183471_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href='/Writing/183698?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄汉阳赵尉沔<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183698")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183698_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183698_0'>① 赵字道原，滂之从兄。丙子十月江夏赋</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183698'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183698'>庆湖遗老坐诗穷，强仕之年百病攻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183698'>谁谓南昌禄隐翁，伏枕呻吟四壁空。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183698'>相思限此江西东，寄声每托江头风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183698'>斯言近俳聊一笑，江水方清饥可疗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183698'>人生奇偶类探筹，造物岂容人数料。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183698'>君初试吏或当然，我太半生真不调。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183698'>昔不愿起家百日登三司，今不愿还家六印金累累。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183698'>但愿官粮办亲养，归来尚馀三径资。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183698'>邻墙晏起访安否，尔酌我歌尧舜时。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183698'>咄嗟此愿良难必，吞声食檗甘如蜜。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_183698'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_183698_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183597' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183597' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183597?labeling=true' target='_blank'>怀寄周元翁十首<span class='inlineComment2'>（丙子十月江夏赋）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183597")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183597_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183597'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183597'>周郎假沔官，我偶来沔居。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183597'>得闲定相过，谈笑沈痾袪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183597'>俄闻戍楼角，晓引吹咿呜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183597'>自君居湓城，恍恍一梦馀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183597'>复求若辈人，陶灶搜璠玙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183597'>诚为天下士，岂特江汉无。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183597'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_183597_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183598' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183598' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183598?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183598'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183598'>周郎嗜茗饮，偶与吾好同。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183598'>赠行发吾宝，紫璧雕云龙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183598'>此实太官物，分甘玉堂公。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183598'>我曹百石吏，藜菽每不充。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183598'>诗人盍得尝，可以骄万钟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183598'>愿君间一歠，千里共清风。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183598'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_183598_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183602' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183602' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183602?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183602_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183602'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183602'>周郎尘外人，冰甃立寒玉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183602'>去我千里馀，炯炯长在目。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183602'>有德且有言，可采篆缣竹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183602'>未为造物怜，方徇斗筲禄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183602'>司晨属群鸡，安事彼鸾鹄。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183602'>聊自况疲驽，盐车不为辱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183602'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_183602_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183601' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183601' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183601?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183601_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183601'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183601'>周郎妙雅道，五字可人师。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183601'>许与非不严，奈何取我诗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183601'>我诗如秋虫，徒增长年悲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183601'>指疵固有望，逐臭得无嗤。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183601'>诗鸣人必穷，我穷岂所宜。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183601'>愿君勿阂此，晚节益经奇。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183601_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183601'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_183601_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183606?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183606'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183606'>周郎归濂溪，旱燥害嘉谷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183606'>仰饱百指馀，嗷然坐空屋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183606'>应书乞米帖，得继朝来粥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183606'>行升大夫籍，月赐万钱禄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183606'>振显属他年，盘飧罗海陆。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183606'>毋忘佛子言，不食大夫福。<div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183600' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183600?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span id='poem_sentence_0_183600'>周郎西笑时，叠寄两函书。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183600'>情亲语恳到，骨肉所不如。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183600'>妙翰骋遒放，抵突黄与苏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183600'>黄癯曳羸筋，苏厚凝腯肤。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183600'>我于季孟间，增少损有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183600'>家鸡敢复道，储此橐中珠。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183600_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183600'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_183600_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183605' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183605' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_183605_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183605'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183605'>周郎走王都，马足尘翻波。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183605'>贺老宦江夏，无人惊雀罗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183605'>出处躁静间，奈此贫病何。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183605'>平生解指誓，晚境忽婆娑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183605'>迫死不得休，前言食已多。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183605_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183599' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183599' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183599?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183599'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183599'>周郎强仕年，药石甘苦口。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183599'>得无耗天和，汤剂御衰朽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183599'>空华与□色，种种竟何有。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183599'>妄爱温柔乡，荡然不回首。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183599'>坐令<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>松桂姿，凋脆等蒲柳。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183599'>幸勿易斯言，前车镜湖叟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183599'></div><div id='poem_note_183599_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_183603' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183603' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183603?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span id='poem_content_183603'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183603'>周郎有史才，班马可并驱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183603'>纷纷谗谄人，畏君笔削诛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183603'>我恨接君晚，要亦君之徒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183603'>沈痾积岁月，顾此留须臾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183603'>志我圹中石，赖君文不谀。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183603'>庶乎陵谷变，名字见君书。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183603'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_183603_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183604' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183604' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183604?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183604_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183604'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183604'>周郎贯江华，而复厌湖湘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183604'>我亦非乐此，西归计茫茫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183604'>颓年抱沈痼，生理岂得长。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183604'>后期真何时，存殁两莫忘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183604'>怀君辄赋诗，落笔联十章。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183604'>它年一掩卷，为我涕浪浪。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183604'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_183604_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_183750' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183750' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183750?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题武昌郑判官直节亭<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183750")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_183750_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183750_0'>① 郑名深，字文通，植竹开亭于官舍东南隅，名直节以自况。丙子十月落成求诗，为赋</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183750'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183750'>开亭榜直节，宠尔青琅玕。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183750_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183750'>岁晚傲霜雪，不同天下寒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183750_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183750'>挺立百丈夫，被之古衣冠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183750_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183750'>春华白粉泽，正色莫敢干。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183750_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183750'>越客与登览，微吟复长叹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183750_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183750'>六鳌方抃戏，云海翻狂澜。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183750_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183750'>傥逢龙伯公，何惮剪一竿。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183750_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183750'>岐山鸣凤雏，久刷五色翰。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183750_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183750'>何以慰朝饥，美实来加餐。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183750_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183750'>高材陋时用，自持良独难。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183750_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_183750'>不<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>愿裁乐管，伶伦非古官。<div id='poem_sentence_10_183750_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年12月</a>　是年十二月,在江夏,有诗。作品：《江夏寓兴二首》之一。《送武庠归隐终南》<div id='poem_247377' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_247377' class='poemTitle id='poem_content_183663'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183663'>君不见南朝豪俊有郗生，自厌出身时网婴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_183663'>一官换得今是翁，昔何所缚今谁解。<div id='poem_sentence_9_183663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年6月</a>　是年六月,在江夏,有诗。作品：《送鄂州刑狱掾王懋元功罢官还海陵兼简金陵和上人》<div id='poem_183670' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183670' class='poemTitle class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_183192_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183192_0'>① 祖字子元，元和乙亥年过吾家外监，授丹及诀，后六十年始化去，寿九十五。门人许鼎为其理（清抄本、四库本作埋）铭，载季真天台升仙事甚详。后为瓦官残子元墓，棺已空矣。此铭今在天庆观中</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183192'><div class='poemSentence' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183575' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183575?labeling=true' target='_blank'>玉钩环歌<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span 诸王孙士泞澄源，以苍玉环螳螂钩见贶，助饰野服。因以珉玉盘、博山炉、成氏箭、建盏、龙茶五物并此歌为报。丁丑十月江夏赋</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183575'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183575'>良工得玉蓝溪窟，相璞命形心匠出。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183575'>螳螂倔彊<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：平）</span>疑有骨，颈系一环犹莫屈。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183575'>镜湖老狂厌袍笏，素裰纁绦须此物。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183575'>价比连城不容乞，王孙辍好人所难。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183575'>何以报之明月盘，薰炉波面山巑岏。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183575'>吾乡美笴鹍鸡翰，闽瓷兔碗霜毛寒。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183575'>称是头贡双龙团，聊送公斋增冗长。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183575'>短歌粗可评珍贶，吾方野装事游放。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_183575'>跼步臞颜曳藜杖，薄暮微吟江汉上。<div id='poem_sentence_8_183575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183666'>送君一樽酒，孤饮聊耳热。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183666'>会取屈平书，商声歌九阕。<div id='poem_title_183502_0'>① 吴字达夫，与吾为忘年之友。兼示慎献玉，故有落句。丁丑十一月赋</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183502'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183502'>城隅黄鹤莫登临，端使悲翁动楚吟。<div "poem_title_183402")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_183402_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183402'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183402'>白云蒙山头，清川山下流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183402_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183402'>芳洲采香女，薄暮漾归舟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183402'>持情不得语，大妇在高楼<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《庆湖遗老诗集》卷四）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183402_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年5月</a>　是年五月,在江夏,有诗。作品：《登黄鹤楼怀古兼寄潘邠老昆仲》<div id='poem_183542' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183542' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_183542_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183542_0'>① 豳老弟大观，字仲达。（四库本作远）戊寅五月赋</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183542'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183542'>汉大将军楚国材，半生倦韵浼尘埃。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183542'>徐夫人匕首安在，丁令威华表归来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183542'>紫府无踪劳彷像，白云有待久裴徊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183542'>楼标空阔天垠<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作根）</span>露，川势从横地纽<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>开。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183542'>陇鸟赋成洲共永，越人歌断棹先回。<div id='poem_title_183758_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_183758_0'>① 潘豳老昆仲躬耕于东坡，葺亦颜斋以偃息，求诗于我，为赋之。元符戊寅六月江夏作</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183758'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183758'>东坡有田谁料理，黧面苍毛潘氏子。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183758'>结茅题榜亦颜斋，农隙把书聊自喜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183758'>潘乎潘乎信是颜之徒，终日何所论难真如愚。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183758'>世无孔父四科友，犹办箪食瓢饮陋巷环墙居。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183758'>百亩之收粒可数，天南有待东坡主。<div id='poem_sentence_4_183758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_183758'>更输什一补官仓，馀勺几何供雀鼠。<div id='poem_sentence_5_183758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_183758'>会须不改其乐媚而翁，力田水旱由天公。<div id='poem_sentence_6_183758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_183758'>大胜心迹相违阮校尉，东西南北哭途穷<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《庆湖遗老诗集》卷一）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_183758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183330'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183330'>仲宣何遽向荆州，谢惠连须更<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作臾）</span>少留。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183330_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183330'>二日旧传挑菜节，一樽聊解负薪忧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183330_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
杭州（钱塘）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f329c8b8859d4728a5354def4706414d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f329c8b8859d4728a5354def4706414d");'><span id='f329c8b8859d4728a5354def4706414d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>，50岁</div><div id='f329c8b8859d4728a5354def4706414d' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>是岁,客寓杭州,观钱塘海潮,有诗。作品：《钱塘海潮》<div id='poem_183465' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_183465' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183465?labeling=true' target='_blank'>钱塘海潮</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183465")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_183465_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183465'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183465'>高岸如陵累石顽，一支涨海横中间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183465_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183465'>九军雷鼓震玉垒，万里墨云驱雪山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183465_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183465'>秦政维舟羞胆怯，史迁舐笔恨才悭。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183465_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183465'>钱郎几许英雄气，强弩三千拟射还。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183465_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_183465'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_183465_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='bd088f8987f94c8cac1aa3e6b230bd2f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bd088f8987f94c8cac1aa3e6b230bd2f");'><span id='bd088f8987f94c8cac1aa3e6b230bd2f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1112')">1111-1112年</a>，60-61岁</div><div id='bd088f8987f94c8cac1aa3e6b230bd2f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年</a><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　是年,张耒卒,六十一岁。<br /></div>

苏州

id='poem_sentence_1_183820'>同来何事不同归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183820'>梧桐半死清霜后，头白鸳鸯失伴飞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_183820_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_183820'>原上草，露初晞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_183820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' showDetail'><a href='/Writing/183309?labeling=true' target='_blank'>铸年五十八因病废得旨休致一绝寄呈姑苏毗陵诸友</a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(32277, "北宋", "贺铸", "poem_title_183309")'>贺铸</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_183309_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_183309'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_183309'>求田问舍向吴津，欲著衰残老病身。<div id='poem_sentence_0_183309_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_183309'>未拜君恩赐剡曲，归来且醉鉴湖春<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_183309_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_183309'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_183309_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_183309'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_183309_0'>⑴ 自注：铸六代祖广平郡王，在五代间久从宣祖皇帝游，因纳女事太祖皇帝，封孝惠皇后，赐第在开封隆和里。当时宣祖、太祖、太宗潜在邸中，每喜饮臣家酒。后来铸高祖六宅使，尝一日预内宴，因（清抄本、四库本作内）有旨宣（原缺，据清抄本、四库本补）索，遂进旧酒并酿法，就赐名鉴湖春。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_183309_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='2a93cde037e14c45917bc36418a063c4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2a93cde037e14c45917bc36418a063c4");'><span id='2a93cde037e14c45917bc36418a063c4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年</a>，58岁</div><div id='2a93cde037e14c45917bc36418a063c4' class='detail'><span
